The Inter Pre-school Competition of drawing and fancy dress was accomplished successfully with the inspiration of Mr. Rajnikant Shah, President Of Royal International School and the Director of Inter-School Drawing and Fancy Dress Association.',  For, the fir', ...', st time in Dombivli such type of competition was held in which around 25 pre-schools had participated in this competition with their mentor, teacher and parents. We have received tremendous response from all the schools participating and also for the free Dental Checkup by Ceramco Dental Clinic was conducted in our school with workshop on oral Health by Dr. Nitin Joshi .',  The competition was inaugurated by the Famous Cinema Actor, Mr. Ashok Kulkarni, who has currently played the role of great Justice Ranade in the famous Marathi movie, Lokmanya Tilak. The judges who judged this competition along with Mr. Ashok Kulkarni were Mr. Amardeep Sawant, who is an Art Instructor and Cinema Artist and also Mr. Sandeep Parab, who is into Serial Editing Department. Mr. Nitin Joshi also gave his precious presence for this auspicious programme.',  For this programme, Mrs. Sumedha Mestry, the principal of Royal International School gave proper guidance to all the programme incharges and has also encouraged the students participating in this programme. Approximately around 510 students participated in Drawing Competition and 275 students participated in fancy dress. Attractive Prizes were given to all the students like Tri-cycles, Bycycles, Trophies and Certificates.',  The main objective of this programme was to develop artistic skills and help the students to develop their talent and prepare them to face the challenges of present day competitive world.',  This programme was thereby accomplished and celebrated with great joy and enthusiasm. We have been more social these days on social media pages across Google +, Faceb...', Continue reading', +3', Royal International School',  added ', 2 new photos',  \u2014 in ', Dombivali East', .',   ', 25 February 2015',   ', Pre-school Balmahotsav : Inter-school Competition of Pre-primary Students held on 10th Jan 2015', Royal International School',   ', 25 February 2015',   ', Royal International School, Dombivli',  10th Jan 2015',  Dombivali Yuvak Education Trust \u2013 Royal International School (CBSE) conducted inter-school competition of Pre-primary students under the banner of \u201cPre-school Balmahotsav\u201d. The Inter Pre-school Competition of drawing and fancy dress was accomplished successfully with the inspiration of Mr. Rajnikant Shah, President Of Royal International School and the Director of Inter-School Drawing and Fancy Dress Association.',  For, the fir', ...', st time in Dombivli such type of competition was held in which around 25 pre-schools had participated in this competition with their mentor, teacher and parents. We have received tremendous response from all the schools participating and also for the free Dental Checkup by Ceramco Dental Clinic was conducted in our school with workshop on oral Health by Dr. Nitin Joshi .',  The competition was inaugurated by the Famous Cinema Actor, Mr. Ashok Kulkarni, who has currently played the role of great Justice Ranade in the famous Marathi movie, Lokmanya Tilak. The judges who judged this competition along with Mr. Ashok Kulkarni were Mr. Amardeep Sawant, who is an Art Instructor and Cinema Artist and also Mr. Sandeep Parab, who is into Serial Editing Department. Mr. Nitin Joshi also gave his precious presence for this auspicious programme.',  For this programme, Mrs. Sumedha Mestry, the principal of Royal International School gave proper guidance to all the programme incharges and has also encouraged the students participating in this programme. Approximately around 510 students participated in Drawing Competition and 275 students participated in fancy dress. Attractive Prizes were given to all the students like Tri-cycles, Bycycles, Trophies and Certificates.',  The main objective of this programme was to develop artistic skills and help the students to develop their talent and prepare them to face the challenges of present day competitive world.',  This programme was thereby accomplished and celebrated with great joy and enthusiasm.
